31  import java.nio.charset.Charset;
32  import java.nio.charset.CharsetDecoder;
33  import java.nio.charset.CharsetEncoder;
34  import java.nio.charset.CharacterCodingException;
35  import sun.nio.cs.HistoricallyNamedCharset;
36  import sun.nio.cs.ext.*;
37  
38  public class IBM1381_OLD
39      extends Charset
40      implements HistoricallyNamedCharset
41  {
42  
43      public IBM1381_OLD() {
44          super("x-IBM1381-Old", null);
45      }
46  
47      public String historicalName() {
48          return "Cp1381";
49      }
50  
51      public boolean contains(Charset cs) {
52          return (cs instanceof IBM1381);
53      }
54  
55      public CharsetDecoder newDecoder() {
56          return new Decoder(this);
57      }
58  
59      public CharsetEncoder newEncoder() {
60          return new Encoder(this);
61      }
62  
63  
64      /**
65       * These accessors are temporarily supplied while sun.io
66       * converters co-exist with the sun.nio.cs.{ext} charset coders
67       * These facilitate sharing of conversion tables between the
68       * two co-existing implementations. When sun.io converters
69       * are made extinct these will be unncessary and should be removed
70       */
71  
72      public String getDecoderSingleByteMappings() {
73          return Decoder.singleByteToChar;
74  
75      }
76  
77      public short[] getDecoderIndex1() {
78          return Decoder.index1;
79      }
80  
81      public String getDecoderIndex2() {
82          return Decoder.index2;
83  
84      }
85  
86      public short[] getEncoderIndex1() {
87          return Encoder.index1;
88  
89      }
90      public String getEncoderIndex2() {
91          return Encoder.index2;
92  
93      }
94      public String getEncoderIndex2a() {
95          return Encoder.index2a;
96  
97      }
98  
99      protected static class Decoder extends DBCS_IBM_ASCII_Decoder {
100 
101         public Decoder(Charset cs) {
102                 super(cs);
103                 super.mask1 = 0xFFE0;
104                 super.mask2 = 0x001F;
105                 super.shift = 5;
106                 super.singleByteToChar = this.singleByteToChar;
107                 super.leadByte = this.leadByte;
108                 super.index1 = this.index1;
109                 super.index2 = this.index2;
110         }
111
